32482  So, in summary, the ffmpeg command takes four input images and applies a blend effect to transition between each image over time. The blend effect creates a smooth transition from one image to the next, making it appear as if the images are zooming in or out. The output video has a resolution of 1280x720 pixels and an aspect ratio of -aspect 3:4, creating a widescreen format. The duration of the transition between each image is set to 1.5 seconds. The final output is saved as outWithFasterBlend.mp4.

INFO Found Here:
 2 
FFmpeg command format
The basic format is: ffmpeg -i originalvideo.mp4 -ss 0:0:4 -t 0:1:10 -vcodec copy -acodec copy outputvideo.mp4
    -ss : start time. If omitted, ffmpeg will start from the beginning
    -t : length in H[H]:M[M]:S[S]

INFO Found Here:
 654 
To Flip Video Vertically
Use the command line to vertically flip the video.
ffmpeg -i INPUT.mp4 -vf vflip -c:a copy OUTPUT.mp4
Step#2: To Flip Video Horizontally
Input following command line to ffmpeg flip video horizontally.
ffmpeg -i INPUT.mp4 -vf hflip -c:a copy OUTPUT.mp4
